126→func (s *Snapshotter) loadMatching(matchFn func(*raftpb.Snapshot) bool) (*raftpb.Snapshot, error) {\n   127→\tnames, err := s.snapNames()\n   128→\tif err != nil {\n   129→\t\treturn nil, err\n snapname string) (*raftpb.Snapshot, error) {\n   157→\tverify.Assert(lg != nil, \"the logger should not be nil\")\n   158→\tb, err := os.ReadFile(snapname)\n   159→\tif err != nil {\n   160→\t\tlg.Warn(\"failed to read a snap file\", zap.String(\"path\", snapname), zap.Error(err))\n   161→\t\treturn nil, err\n   162→\t}\n   163→\n   164→\tif len(b) == 0 {\n   165→\t\tlg.Warn(\"failed logical time order (from newest to oldest).\n   199→// If there is no available snapshots, an ErrNoSnapshot will be returned.\n   200→func (s *Snapshotter) snapNames() ([]string, error) {\n   201→\tdir, err := os.Open(s.dir)\n   202→\tif err != nil {\n   203→\t\treturn nil, err\n   204→\t}\n   205→\tdefer dir.Close()\n   206→\tnames, err := dir.Readdirnames(-1)\n   207→\tif err != nil {\n *Snapshotter) checkSuffix(names []string) []string {\n   223→\tvar snaps []string\n   224→\tfor i := range names {\n   225→\t\tif strings.HasSuffix(names[i], snapSuffix) {\n   226→\t\t\tsnaps = Definition\n\nErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable is returned by the Storage interface when the required snapshot is temporarily unavailable.\n\n## Purpose\n\nIf snapshot is temporarily unavailable, it should return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable, so raft state machine could know that Storage needs some time to prepare snapshot and call Snapshot later.\n\n## Known Issue\n\nThere was a bug reported in the etcd-io/raft project where MemoryStorage.Snapshot does not return ErrSnapshotTemporarilyUnavailable when snapshot is nil.
